  • texlive-xintsession - Interactive computing sessions (fractions, floating points, polynomials)
  • texlive-xmuthesis - XMU thesis style
  • texlive-zbmath-review-template - Template for a zbMATH Open review
  • texlive-zztex - A full-featured TeX macro package for producing books, journals, and manuals
  • texlive-ketcindy - macros for graphic generation and Cinderella plugin
